        SELECT [u].[Id], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[Email], [u].[FirstName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[LastName], [u].[OrganizationId], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[Phone], [u].[RefreshToken], [u].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u].[Role], [u].[SelectedClinicId], [u].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Users] AS [u]
    ) AS [u0] ON [p].[UserId] = [u0].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__request_Id_0 AND [p].[OrganizationId] = @__organizationId_1
) AS [s]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[ClinicId], [a].[CreatedAt], [a].[DoctorId], [a].[IsActive], [a].[Notes], [a].[OrganizationId], [a].[PatientId], [a].[Status], [a].[TokenNumber], [a].[Type], [a].[UpdatedAt], [a].[AppointmentDate], [d0].[Id] AS [Id0], [d0].[BaseClinicId], [d0].[ConsultationFeeInPerson], [d0].[ConsultationFeeTele], [d0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [d0].[ExperienceYears], [d0].[FollowupFeeInPerson], [d0].[FollowupFeeTele], [d0].[IsActive] AS [IsActive0], [d0].[OrganizationId] AS [OrganizationId0], [d0].[Qualification], [d0].[RegistrationNumber], [d0].[Specialization], [d0].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0], [d0].[UserId], [u2].[Id] AS [Id1], [u2].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt1], [u2].[Email], [u2].[FirstName], [u2].[IsActive] AS [IsActive1], [u2].[LastName], [u2].[OrganizationId] AS [OrganizationId1], [u2].[PasswordHash], [u2].[Phone], [u2].[RefreshToken], [u2].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u2].[Role], [u2].[SelectedClinicId], [u2].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt1], [c0].[Id] AS [Id2], [c0].[Address], [c0].[Code], [c0].[ContactEmail], [c0].[ContactPhone], [c0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt2], [c0].[EveningEndTime], [c0].[EveningStartTime], [c0].[FullDayEndTime], [c0].[FullDayStartTime], [c0].[IsActive] AS [IsActive2], [c0].[MorningEndTime], [c0].[MorningStartTime], [c0].[Name], [c0].[OperatingHoursType], [c0].[OrganizationId] AS [OrganizationId2], [c0].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt2]
    FROM [Appointments] AS [a]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[BaseClinicId], [d].[ConsultationFeeInPerson], [d].[ConsultationFeeTele], [d].[CreatedAt], [d].[ExperienceYears], [d].[FollowupFeeInPerson], [d].[FollowupFeeTele], [d].[IsActive], [d].[OrganizationId], [d].[Qualification], [d].[RegistrationNumber], [d].[Specialization], [d].[UpdatedAt], [d].[UserId]
        FROM [DoctorProfiles] AS [d]
    ) AS [d0] ON [a].[DoctorId] = [d0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [u1].[Id], [u1].[CreatedAt], [u1].[Email], [u1].[FirstName], [u1].[IsActive], [u1].[LastName], [u1].[OrganizationId], [u1].[PasswordHash], [u1].[Phone], [u1].[RefreshToken], [u1].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u1].[Role], [u1].[SelectedClinicId], [u1].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Users] AS [u1]
    ) AS [u2] ON [d0].[UserId] = [u2].[Id]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[Address], [c].[Code], [c].[ContactEmail], [c].[ContactPhone], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[EveningEndTime], [c].[EveningStartTime], [c].[FullDayEndTime], [c].[FullDayStartTime], [c].[IsActive], [c].[MorningEndTime], [c].[MorningStartTime], [c].[Name], [c].[OperatingHoursType], [c].[OrganizationId], [c].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Clinics] AS [c]
    ) AS [c0] ON [a].[ClinicId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [s0] ON [s].[Id] = [s0].[PatientId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[Id], [c1].[AppointmentId], [c1].[ChiefComplaint], [c1].[ConsultationDate], [c1].[ConsultationFee], [c1].[CreatedAt], [c1].[Diagnosis], [c1].[DoctorId], [c1].[Examination], [c1].[IsActive], [c1].[Notes], [c1].[OrganizationId], [c1].[PatientId], [c1].[Symptoms], [c1].[TreatmentPlan], [c1].[UpdatedAt], [d2].[Id] AS [Id0], [d2].[BaseClinicId], [d2].[ConsultationFeeInPerson], [d2].[ConsultationFeeTele], [d2].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [d2].[ExperienceYears], [d2].[FollowupFeeInPerson], [d2].[FollowupFeeTele], [d2].[IsActive] AS [IsActive0], [d2].[OrganizationId] AS [OrganizationId0], [d2].[Qualification], [d2].[RegistrationNumber], [d2].[Specialization], [d2].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0], [d2].[UserId], [u4].[Id] AS [Id1], [u4].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt1], [u4].[Email], [u4].[FirstName], [u4].[IsActive] AS [IsActive1], [u4].[LastName], [u4].[OrganizationId] AS [OrganizationId1], [u4].[PasswordHash], [u4].[Phone], [u4].[RefreshToken], [u4].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u4].[Role], [u4].[SelectedClinicId], [u4].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt1], [p1].[Id] AS [Id2], [p1].[ConsultationId], [p1].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt2], [p1].[InternalNotes], [p1].[IsActive] AS [IsActive2], [p1].[IssuedDate], [p1].[OrganizationId] AS [OrganizationId2], [p1].[PatientInstructions], [p1].[PrescriptionNumber], [p1].[Status], [p1].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt2]
    FROM [Consultations] AS [c1]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [d1].[Id], [d1].[BaseClinicId], [d1].[ConsultationFeeInPerson], [d1].[ConsultationFeeTele], [d1].[CreatedAt], [d1].[ExperienceYears], [d1].[FollowupFeeInPerson], [d1].[FollowupFeeTele], [d1].[IsActive], [d1].[OrganizationId], [d1].[Qualification], [d1].[RegistrationNumber], [d1].[Specialization], [d1].[UpdatedAt], [d1].[UserId]
        FROM [DoctorProfiles] AS [d1]
    ) AS [d2] ON [c1].[DoctorId] = [d2].[Id]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [u3].[Id], [u3].[CreatedAt], [u3].[Email], [u3].[FirstName], [u3].[IsActive], [u3].[LastName], [u3].[OrganizationId], [u3].[PasswordHash], [u3].[Phone], [u3].[RefreshToken], [u3].[RefreshTokenExpiryTime], [u3].[Role], [u3].[SelectedClinicId], [u3].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Users] AS [u3]
    ) AS [u4] ON [d2].[UserId] = [u4].[Id]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[ConsultationId], [p0].[CreatedAt], [p0].[InternalNotes], [p0].[IsActive], [p0].[IssuedDate], [p0].[OrganizationId], [p0].[PatientInstructions], [p0].[PrescriptionNumber], [p0].[Status], [p0].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Prescriptions] AS [p0]
    ) AS [p1] ON [c1].[Id] = [p1].[ConsultationId]
) AS [s1] ON [s].[Id] = [s1].[PatientId]
ORDER BY [s].[Id], [s].[Id0], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0], [s0].[Id1], [s0].[Id2], [s1].[Id], [s1].[Id0], [s1].[Id1]
